[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The nested loops in CellFormatter.format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m67[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m75[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m use denomLength = mask [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to [0m[1;36m20[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, then compute fullMaxDenominator = [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^denomLength – [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39miterate i from fullMaxDenominator down to [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, and i2 from fullMaxDenominator down to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m. For [0m[33mdenomLength[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m this is effectively [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m^[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m iterations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhuge, causing the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhang[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Although the regex caps mask length to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m, there is no guard on the work done;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madversarial inputs easily trigger this denial-of-service loop.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Strategy to Fix[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Introduce a safe upper bound [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconstant[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on the maximum denominator considered [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the brute-force search to cap work in all cases. This preserves correct behavior[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor typical masks but prevents DoS for large masks.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not modify the regex or harness; only patch CellFormatter.format.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Steps to Implement[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In CellFormatter, define a new static constant, for example:[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        private static final int MAX_DENOMINATOR_LIMIT = [0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m([0m[39mThis cap ensures at most ~[0m[1;36m1e6[0m[39m iterations—safe in practice.[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. After extracting denomFormat and computing denomLength, compute:[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        double fullMaxDenominator = [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        int maxDenominator = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35mMath.min[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfullMaxDenominator, [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_DENOMINATOR_LIMIT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      Replace any direct use of [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, denomLength[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - 1d[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaxDenominator.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Adjust the nested loops to:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i = maxDenominator; i > [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint i2 = maxDenominator; i2 >= [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i2--[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m               [0m[33m...[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Optionally, break early if an exact match [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdiff == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is found:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mminVal == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m break outerLoop;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      to further reduce average work.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Preservation[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach ensures that for reasonable masks [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., mask length ≤ [0m[1;36m3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, full [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrute-force is applied exactly as before. For larger masks, the work is simply [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcapped to a safe constant.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing formatting logic and API remain unchanged; only the iteration bounds [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchange.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing tests and fuzz harness continue operating; no changes to parser [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloops or test code.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very large masks [0m[1;39m([0m[39m> ~[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m digits[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now only search denominators up to [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_DENOMINATOR_LIMIT. Their fraction output may be less precise than before but [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoids DoS.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If downstream code relies on extremely large denominators [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely in CSV [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mformatting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, increase MAX_DENOMINATOR_LIMIT conservatively or implement a more [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mefficient continued-fraction algorithm.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We preserve the fallback to decimal formatting when no FRACTION_FORMAT match [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis found.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar capping patterns exist elsewhere in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., limiting [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteger and fraction precision via regex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This patch applies a corresponding [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruntime bound to prevent excessive computation.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
